Fishing Notebook
Fish Glossary
     Time Trial
 Back
  Rod
  Reel & Line
 Lure
Japanese mountain streamwith everything from    native to transplanted  fish. Even a beginner   can enjoy the thrill of a catch using lures     ranging from a minnow   plug to a spoon.
River near its source innorthern country valley.Native trout, attracted by insects falling from surrounding trees, make this an ideal fishing   spot. The best casting  points are the deep and the rocky areas.
Stocked with numerous   fish, this lake is a    breeding ground for bassand trout. A popular    site, it attracts many  enthusiasts, making it  difficult for any big   catches. Ideal for      beginners.
An agricultural-use     reservoir formed from   the water surplus of    local river improvement projects. Fish are      farmed in the reservoir,and it is stocked with  black bass. A favorite  spot for bass anglers.
Artificial lake created for a dam project. Home to black bass and       bluegills, the lake is  a site for some record  catches. The areas near the bordering trees are the target points of    this lake. 
A river on the western  coast of the U.S. that  features several king   salmon which gather     there prior to spawning.Casting accuracy isn't  necessary. The main     concern is how to land  the powerful salmon.
Located near the Rocky  Mountains, this river isknown for the steelheadsthat migrate upstream.  Casting near bridge     pilings where the trout gather in pursuit of    baitfish can result in  trophy-size catches.
A crystal-clear lake    with water supplied fromthe melted snow of      nearby mountains. The   numerous fish that      live in this cold       environment are known   for their firm meat.
This river is home to   Australia's massive gamefish, Barramunda. In    theory, the best        approach is to focus on the top water and use a noisy lure.
North Island's Tongariroriver is abundant with  life forms that gather  around the reeds. Known for its well-shaped     trout, it's a favorite  spot for anglers.
The middle of a river   located on grazing land in the South Island.    Trout gather to feed on the insects that fall   from the nearby grass.  Free of predators, this is the best fishing spotfor large brown trout.
A large South American  river teeming with life.Patience is usually     rewarded with some of   the world's largest gamefish. The plants that   float on the water's    surface do not always   hide large catches.
A water area surrounded by dense jungle. This isa challenging spot that requires good technique.A poorly selected lure  will only attract the   local piranhas.
A vast, boggy region in Brazil. This area is    said to be the home of  a legendary fish that   shines like gold. The   name of whoever catches this fish will be       forever remembered amonganglers.
A member of the Iwana   family, this fish can befound in Japan's        Hokkaido and Northern   Honshu regions. The fishhas a beautiful silver  body speckled with dots.It mainly feeds on      insects and small fish.
Born without its normal pigment, this is a rare and beautiful variation of the rainbow trout.
Found in South America, this yellow-colored     piranha can be found    throughout the Amazon   River region. Like the  rest of the piranha     family, this fish is    ferocious as well as    aggressive.
Opposed to the Yamame,  the Iwana is considered masculine. The fish can be found in the mountainstreams of Japan. The   Iwana feeds on insects  and smaller fish. It    prefers lower water     temperatures and gentle currents.
Native to China, this isa greedy fish that feedsnot only on small fish, but also on frogs and   snakes. A rough fighter,this fish can be found  in shallow, stagnant    water areas that are    heavy with plants.
This king of trout      migrates between the seaand rivers of North     America. Among salmons, it is known for its     longevity, and is the   longest in terms of     length. Delicious in    flavor, it is a very    popular game fish.
Native to South America,this freshwater fish is known to grow to        significant sizes. Knownas a man-eating catfish,records show that it hasswallowed a child in thepast. This fish is very aggressive in nature.
This is the saltwater   version of the Rainbow  Trout. Known to reach a maximum length of over  1 meter, this shiny     silver fighter is a     favorite challenge amonganglers.
Native to South America,this fish is recognized from its lovely stripes.Usually found in the    shallows where the      current is strong, it   primarily feeds on smallfish and shells. It is  also a popular fish for aquariums.
Also known as peacock   bass, this fish is      recognized by anglers   worldwide as an intense top water fighter. The  fish is often found in  the shallows along a    river.
A golden fish that is   native to Pantanal. It  swims along the shore topursue smaller fish. A  strong fighter, it is   considered to be South  America's top game fish.
Found almost anywhere inJapan, this fish is     known to hide at the    bottom of the water and strikes out at anything that moves. In Japan,   legend has it that this fish is able to predict earthquakes.
This fish can be found  in the cold regions of  North America. With     its distinct features,  this fish is known as a game fish equal to bass or trout. It feeds on   fish near the bottom of the water and is seldom seen at top water.
The pride of Australia, this large fish is a    very difficult catch andprime target areas are  limited. Lures with     strong appeal are       particularly effective. Highly aggressive, the  fish is capable of      snapping lighter lines.
Native to Northern      Europe, this trout gets its name from the light brown color of its body.Much more wary than the rainbow trout, this is adifficult fish to catch.For best results, use   minnow or spoon-type    metal lures.
Native to South America,this is the fish that isusually referred to whenpiranhas are mentioned. When food is in short   supply, these fish are  known to aggressively   feed on each other.
This is the world's     largest class of        freshwater fish. It is  beautiful fish that     turns scarlet as it     matures. There is no    record of this fish     being landed by means oflure fishing.
This is a very popular  and famous game fish. Anintense fighter, it is  known to determinedly   attack noisy lures.     Native to North America,it prefers to hide in   water areas containing  plants and other        obstacles.
A member of the piranha species found in South  America. One of the     larger of the species,  this fish is vicious andwill bite just about    anything that wanders   nearby.
A member of the sunfish species, this fish growsto about 20cm in length.Though fairly small, thefish is a fighter that  is widely recognized as a challenge among most  anglers. The fish can befound almost anywhere inthe United States.
With a long, thin body  and sizeable canine     teeth, this fish is     capable of easily       crushing any lures that it catches in its jaws.
Described as feminine,  this fish is found in   the mountain streams of Japan. Though known to  spend its lifetime in   the river, those that   reach the sea and matureare called Sakura Masu. This wary fish mainly   feeds on insects.
Representative of the   trout species, this fishderives its name from   the rainbow-colored     pattern along its body. Though the larger of    this variety feed on    other fish, rainbow     trout generally prefer  small bait.
Native to South America,this fish is easily     recognized by its red   tail and is a popular   aquarium fish. Universalto catfish, it has an   extremely good appetite.
